  requires a <= b
  ensures RangeSeq(a, b) == RangeSeq(a, b - 1) + [b]
  decreases b - a

  if a < b { RangeSeqAppend(a + 1, b); }
}

lemma InitialListEqualsRange(n: nat)
  ensures InitialList(n) == RangeSeq(1, n)
  decreases n
{
  if n > 0 {
    InitialListEqualsRange(n - 1);
    RangeSeqAppend(1, n);
  }
}

// Key lemma: simulating from a state [2,4,...,2k] ++ [2k+1,...,n] yields [2,4,...,2*(n/2)]
lemma SimulateFromState(k: nat, n: nat)
  requires 2 * k <= n
  ensures Simulate(EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n), k + 1) == EvenList(n / 2)
  decreases n - 2 * k
{
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(k)
  assert |EvenList(k)| == k;
  RangeSeqLength(2 * k + 1, n);
  var state := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
  if 2 * k == n {
    // Base: range is empty, step > |state|, Simulate returns state
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [];
  } else {
    // Inductive step: 2k < n, so step k+1 is valid
    assert |state| == n - k;
    assert k + 1 <= n - k;
    // Identify what's at index k (first element of the range suffix)
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [2 * k + 1] + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert state[..k] == EvenList(k);
    assert state[k..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
    assert state[k + 1..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    // After removing index k
    var afterRemoval := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert RemoveAtIndex(state, k) == afterRemoval;
    if 2 * (k + 1) > n {
      // n = 2k+1 (odd): range becomes empty
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k);
      assert n / 2 == k;
    } else {
      // 2(k+1) <= n: fold 2k+2 into the even prefix
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [2 * (k + 1)] + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      assert EvenList(k + 1) == EvenList(k) + [2 * (k + 1)];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k + 1) + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      SimulateFromState(k + 1, n);
    }
  }
}

  requires x >= 1
  requires x <= |FinalList(n)|
  ensures result == FinalList(n)[x - 1]

  return x * 2;

ghost function InitialList(n: nat): seq<int>
  decreases n
{
  if n == 0 then [] else InitialList(n - 1) + [n]
}

ghost function RemoveAtIndex(s: seq<int>, idx: nat): seq<int>
  requires idx < |s|
{
  s[..idx] + s[idx + 1..]
}

ghost function Simulate(remaining: seq<int>, step: nat): seq<int>
  decreases |remaining|
{
  if step == 0 || step > |remaining| then remaining
  else Simulate(RemoveAtIndex(remaining, step - 1), step + 1)

ghost function FinalList(n: nat): seq<int>
{
  Simulate(InitialList(n), 1)
}

// --- Proof infrastructure ---

ghost function EvenList(k: nat): seq<int>
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 then [] else EvenList(k - 1) + [2 * k]
}

ghost function RangeSeq(a: int, b: int): seq<int>
  decreases if b >= a then b - a + 1 else 0
{
  if a > b then [] else [a] + RangeSeq(a + 1, b)
}

lemma EvenListElement(k: nat, i: nat)
  requires i < k
  ensures |EvenList(k)| == k
  ensures EvenList(k)[i] == 2 * (i + 1)
  decreases k
{
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(k)
  assert |EvenList(k)| == k;
  if i < k - 1 {
    EvenListElement(k - 1, i);
  }
}

lemma RangeSeqLength(a: int, b: int)
  ensures |RangeSeq(a, b)| == if a > b then 0 else b - a + 1
  decreases if b >= a then b - a + 1 else 0
{
  if a <= b { RangeSeqLength(a + 1, b); }
}

lemma RangeSeqAppend(a: int, b: int)
  requires a <= b
  ensures RangeSeq(a, b) == RangeSeq(a, b - 1) + [b]
  decreases b - a
{
  if a < b { RangeSeqAppend(a + 1, b); }
}

lemma InitialListEqualsRange(n: nat)
  ensures InitialList(n) == RangeSeq(1, n)
  decreases n
{
  if n > 0 {
    InitialListEqualsRange(n - 1);
    RangeSeqAppend(1, n);
  }
}

// Key lemma: simulating from a state [2,4,...,2k] ++ [2k+1,...,n] yields [2,4,...,2*(n/2)]
lemma SimulateFromState(k: nat, n: nat)
  requires 2 * k <= n
  ensures Simulate(EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n), k + 1) == EvenList(n / 2)
  decreases n - 2 * k
{
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(k)
  assert |EvenList(k)| == k;
  RangeSeqLength(2 * k + 1, n);
  var state := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
  if 2 * k == n {
    // Base: range is empty, step > |state|, Simulate returns state
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [];
  } else {
    // Inductive step: 2k < n, so step k+1 is valid
    assert |state| == n - k;
    assert k + 1 <= n - k;
    // Identify what's at index k (first element of the range suffix)
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [2 * k + 1] + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert state[..k] == EvenList(k);
    assert state[k..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
    assert state[k + 1..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    // After removing index k
    var afterRemoval := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert RemoveAtIndex(state, k) == afterRemoval;
    if 2 * (k + 1) > n {
      // n = 2k+1 (odd): range becomes empty
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k);
      assert n / 2 == k;
    } else {
      // 2(k+1) <= n: fold 2k+2 into the even prefix
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [2 * (k + 1)] + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      assert EvenList(k + 1) == EvenList(k) + [2 * (k + 1)];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k + 1) + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      SimulateFromState(k + 1, n);
    }
  }
}

lemma FinalListIsEven(n: nat)
  ensures FinalList(n) == EvenList(n / 2)
{
  InitialListEqualsRange(n);
  SimulateFromState(0, n);
}

method RemoveAProgression(n: int, x: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 1
  requires x >= 1
  requires x <= |FinalList(n)|
  ensures result == FinalList(n)[x - 1]
{
  // Inlined from FinalListIsEven(n)
  InitialListEqualsRange((n));

  SimulateFromState(0, (n));

  // Inlined from EvenListLength(n / 2)

  EvenListElement(n / 2, x - 1);
  return x * 2;
}

  } else {
    // Inductive step: 2k < n, so step k+1 is valid
    assert |state| == n - k;
    assert k + 1 <= n - k;
    // Identify what's at index k (first element of the range suffix)
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [2 * k + 1] + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert state[..k] == EvenList(k);
    assert state[k..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
    assert state[k + 1..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    // After removing index k
    var afterRemoval := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert RemoveAtIndex(state, k) == afterRemoval;
    if 2 * (k + 1) > n {
      // n = 2k+1 (odd): range becomes empty
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k);
      assert n / 2 == k;
      assert EvenList(n / 2) == EvenList(k);
      assert Simulate(afterRemoval, k + 2) == EvenList(k);
    } else {
      // 2(k+1) <= n: fold 2k+2 into the even prefix
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [2 * (k + 1)] + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      assert EvenList(k + 1) == EvenList(k) + [2 * (k + 1)];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k + 1) + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      SimulateFromState(k + 1, n);
    }
  }
}

lemma FinalListIsEven(n: nat)
  ensures FinalList(n) == EvenList(n / 2)
{
  InitialListEqualsRange(n);
  SimulateFromState(0, n);
}

  decreases n

// Key lemma: simulating from a state [2,4,...,2k] ++ [2k+1,...,n] yields [2,4,...,2*(n/2)]
lemma SimulateFromState(k: nat, n: nat)
  requires 2 * k <= n
  ensures Simulate(EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n), k + 1) == EvenList(n / 2)
  decreases n - 2 * k
{
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(k)
  assert |EvenList(k)| == k;
  RangeSeqLength(2 * k + 1, n);
  var state := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
  if 2 * k == n {
    // Base: range is empty, step > |state|, Simulate returns state
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [];
    // state is EvenList(k)
    assert state == EvenList(k);
    // Simulate with step k+1 > |state| returns state
    assert Simulate(state, k + 1) == state;
    // n/2 == k
    assert n / 2 == k;
    // Therefore result equals EvenList(k)
    assert Simulate(state, k + 1) == EvenList(k);
  } else {
    // Inductive step: 2k < n, so step k+1 is valid
    assert |state| == n - k;
    assert k + 1 <= n - k;
    // Identify what's at index k (first element of the range suffix)
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [2 * k + 1] + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert state[..k] == EvenList(k);
    assert state[k..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
    assert state[k + 1..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    // After removing index k
    var afterRemoval := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert RemoveAtIndex(state, k) == afterRemoval;
    if 2 * (k + 1) > n {
      // n = 2k+1 (odd): range becomes empty
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k);
      assert n / 2 == k;
      // Simulate from afterRemoval with step k+2
      assert Simulate(afterRemoval, k + 2) == afterRemoval;
      assert Simulate(state, k + 1) == afterRemoval;
      assert Simulate(state, k + 1) == EvenList(k);
    } else {
      // 2(k+1) <= n: fold 2k+2 into the even prefix
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [2 * (k + 1)] + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      assert EvenList(k + 1) == EvenList(k) + [2 * (k + 1)];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k + 1) + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      // Recursively simulate from the new state
      assert Simulate(afterRemoval, k + 2) == EvenList(n / 2);
      assert Simulate(state, k + 1) == Simulate(afterRemoval, k + 2);
      assert Simulate(state, k + 1) == EvenList(n / 2);
    }
  }
}

  SimulateFromState(0, n);

lemma EvenListElement(k: nat, i: nat)
  requires i < k
  ensures |EvenList(k)| == k
  ensures EvenList(k)[i] == 2 * (i + 1)
  decreases k
{
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(k)
  assert |EvenList(k)| == k;
  if i < k - 1 {
    EvenListElement(k - 1, i);
  }
}

lemma RangeSeqLength(a: int, b: int)
  ensures |RangeSeq(a, b)| == if a > b then 0 else b - a + 1
  decreases if b >= a then b - a + 1 else 0
{
  if a <= b { RangeSeqLength(a + 1, b); }
}

lemma RangeSeqAppend(a: int, b: int)
  requires a <= b
  ensures RangeSeq(a, b) == RangeSeq(a, b - 1) + [b]
  decreases b - a
{
  if a < b { RangeSeqAppend(a + 1, b); }
}

lemma InitialListEqualsRange(n: nat)
  ensures InitialList(n) == RangeSeq(1, n)
  decreases n
{
  if n > 0 {
    InitialListEqualsRange(n - 1);
    RangeSeqAppend(1, n);
  }
}

// Key lemma: simulating from a state [2,4,...,2k] ++ [2k+1,...,n] yields [2,4,...,2*(n/2)]
lemma SimulateFromState(k: nat, n: nat)
  requires 2 * k <= n
  ensures Simulate(EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n), k + 1) == EvenList(n / 2)
  decreases n - 2 * k
{
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(k)
  assert |EvenList(k)| == k;
  RangeSeqLength(2 * k + 1, n);
  var state := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
  if 2 * k == n {
    // Base: range is empty, step > |state|, Simulate returns state
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [];
  } else {
    // Inductive step: 2k < n, so step k+1 is valid
    assert |state| == n - k;
    assert k + 1 <= n - k;
    // Identify what's at index k (first element of the range suffix)
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [2 * k + 1] + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert state[..k] == EvenList(k);
    assert state[k..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
    assert state[k + 1..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    // After removing index k
    var afterRemoval := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert RemoveAtIndex(state, k) == afterRemoval;
    if 2 * (k + 1) > n {
      // n = 2k+1 (odd): range becomes empty
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k);
      assert n / 2 == k;
    } else {
      // 2(k+1) <= n: fold 2k+2 into the even prefix
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [2 * (k + 1)] + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      assert EvenList(k + 1) == EvenList(k) + [2 * (k + 1)];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k + 1) + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      SimulateFromState(k + 1, n);
    }
  }
}

lemma FinalListIsEven(n: nat)
  ensures |FinalList(n)| == n / 2
  ensures forall i :: 0 <= i < |FinalList(n)| ==> FinalList(n)[i] == 2 * (i + 1)
{
  // Inlined from InitialListEqualsRange
  InitialListEqualsRange(n);
  // Inlined from SimulateFromState
  SimulateFromState(0, n);
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(n / 2)
  assert |EvenList(n / 2)| == n / 2;
  // Inlined from EvenListElement
  assert forall i :: 0 <= i < n / 2 ==> EvenList(n / 2)[i] == 2 * (i + 1);
  // Since FinalList(n) == EvenList(n/2)
  assert FinalList(n) == EvenList(n / 2);
}

method RemoveAProgression(n: int, x: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 1
  requires x >= 1
  requires x <= |FinalList(n)|
  ensures result == FinalList(n)[x - 1]
{
  // Inlined from FinalListIsEven(n)
  InitialListEqualsRange(n);
  SimulateFromState(0, n);
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(n / 2)
  assert |EvenList(n / 2)| == n / 2;
  // Inlined from EvenListElement
  EvenListElement(n / 2, x - 1);
  return x * 2;
}

lemma EvenListElement(k: nat, i: nat)
  requires i < k
  ensures |EvenList(k)| == k
  ensures EvenList(k)[i] == 2 * (i + 1)
  decreases k

  if i < k - 1 {
    EvenListElement(k - 1, i);
  }

lemma RangeSeqLength(a: int, b: int)
  ensures |RangeSeq(a, b)| == if a > b then 0 else b - a + 1
  decreases if b >= a then b - a + 1 else 0
{
  if a <= b { RangeSeqLength(a + 1, b); }
}

lemma RangeSeqAppend(a: int, b: int)
  requires a <= b
  ensures RangeSeq(a, b) == RangeSeq(a, b - 1) + [b]
  decreases b - a
{
  if a < b { RangeSeqAppend(a + 1, b); }
}

lemma InitialListEqualsRange(n: nat)
  ensures InitialList(n) == RangeSeq(1, n)
  decreases n
{
  if n > 0 {
    InitialListEqualsRange(n - 1);
    RangeSeqAppend(1, n);
  }
}

// Key lemma: simulating from a state [2,4,...,2k] ++ [2k+1,...,n] yields [2,4,...,2*(n/2)]
lemma SimulateFromState(k: nat, n: nat)
  requires 2 * k <= n
  ensures Simulate(EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n), k + 1) == EvenList(n / 2)
  decreases n - 2 * k
{
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(k)
  assert |EvenList(k)| == k;
  RangeSeqLength(2 * k + 1, n);
  var state := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
  if 2 * k == n {
    // Base: range is empty, step > |state|, Simulate returns state
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [];
  } else {
    // Inductive step: 2k < n, so step k+1 is valid
    assert |state| == n - k;
    assert k + 1 <= n - k;
    // Identify what's at index k (first element of the range suffix)
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [2 * k + 1] + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert state[..k] == EvenList(k);
    assert state[k..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
    assert state[k + 1..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    // After removing index k
    var afterRemoval := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert RemoveAtIndex(state, k) == afterRemoval;
    if 2 * (k + 1) > n {
      // n = 2k+1 (odd): range becomes empty
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k);
      assert n / 2 == k;
    } else {
      // 2(k+1) <= n: fold 2k+2 into the even prefix
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [2 * (k + 1)] + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      assert EvenList(k + 1) == EvenList(k) + [2 * (k + 1)];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k + 1) + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      SimulateFromState(k + 1, n);
    }
  }
}

lemma FinalListIsEven(n: nat)
  ensures EvenList(n / 2) == FinalList(n)
{
  InitialListEqualsRange(n);
  SimulateFromState(0, n);
}

method RemoveAProgression(n: int, x: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 1
  requires x >= 1
  requires x <= |FinalList(n)|
  ensures result == FinalList(n)[x - 1]
{
  // Inlined from FinalListIsEven(n)
  InitialListEqualsRange((n));

  SimulateFromState(0, (n));

  // Inlined from EvenListLength(n / 2)

  EvenListElement(n / 2, x - 1);
  return x * 2;
}

  decreases |remaining|
{
  if step == 0 || step > |remaining| then remaining
  else Simulate(RemoveAtIndex(remaining, step - 1), step + 1)

  Simulate(InitialList(n), 1)

ghost function EvenList(k: nat): seq<int>
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 then [] else EvenList(k - 1) + [2 * k]
}

ghost function RangeSeq(a: int, b: int): seq<int>
  decreases if b >= a then b - a + 1 else 0
{
  if a > b then [] else [a] + RangeSeq(a + 1, b)
}

lemma EvenListElement(k: nat, i: nat)
  requires i < k
  ensures |EvenList(k)| == k
  ensures EvenList(k)[i] == 2 * (i + 1)
  decreases k
{
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(k)
  assert |EvenList(k)| == k;
  if i < k - 1 {
    EvenListElement(k - 1, i);
  }
}

lemma RangeSeqLength(a: int, b: int)
  ensures |RangeSeq(a, b)| == if a > b then 0 else b - a + 1
  decreases if b >= a then b - a + 1 else 0
{
  if a <= b { RangeSeqLength(a + 1, b); }
}

lemma RangeSeqAppend(a: int, b: int)
  requires a <= b
  ensures RangeSeq(a, b) == RangeSeq(a, b - 1) + [b]
  decreases b - a
{
  if a < b { RangeSeqAppend(a + 1, b); }
}

lemma InitialListEqualsRange(n: nat)
  ensures InitialList(n) == RangeSeq(1, n)
  decreases n
{
  if n > 0 {
    InitialListEqualsRange(n - 1);
    RangeSeqAppend(1, n);
  }
}

// Key lemma: simulating from a state [2,4,...,2k] ++ [2k+1,...,n] yields [2,4,...,2*(n/2)]
lemma SimulateFromState(k: nat, n: nat)
  requires 2 * k <= n
  ensures Simulate(EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n), k + 1) == EvenList(n / 2)
  decreases n - 2 * k
{
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(k)
  assert |EvenList(k)| == k;
  RangeSeqLength(2 * k + 1, n);
  var state := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
  if 2 * k == n {
    // Base: range is empty, step > |state|, Simulate returns state
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [];
  } else {
    // Inductive step: 2k < n, so step k+1 is valid
    assert |state| == n - k;
    assert k + 1 <= n - k;
    // Identify what's at index k (first element of the range suffix)
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [2 * k + 1] + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert state[..k] == EvenList(k);
    assert state[k..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
    assert state[k + 1..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    // After removing index k
    var afterRemoval := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert RemoveAtIndex(state, k) == afterRemoval;
    if 2 * (k + 1) > n {
      // n = 2k+1 (odd): range becomes empty
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k);
      assert n / 2 == k;
    } else {
      // 2(k+1) <= n: fold 2k+2 into the even prefix
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [2 * (k + 1)] + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      assert EvenList(k + 1) == EvenList(k) + [2 * (k + 1)];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k + 1) + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      SimulateFromState(k + 1, n);
    }
  }
}

lemma FinalListIsEven(n: nat)
{
  // Not required for verification
}

method RemoveAProgression(n: int, x: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 1
  requires x >= 1
  requires x <= |FinalList(n)|
  ensures result == FinalList(n)[x - 1]
{
  // Inlined from FinalListIsEven(n)
  InitialListEqualsRange((n));

  SimulateFromState(0, (n));

  // Inlined from EvenListLength(n / 2)

  EvenListElement(n / 2, x - 1);
  return x * 2;
}

lemma EvenListElement(k: nat, i: nat)
  requires i < k
  ensures |EvenList(k)| == k
  ensures EvenList(k)[i] == 2 * (i + 1)
  decreases k
{
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(k)
  assert |EvenList(k)| == k;
  if i < k - 1 {
    EvenListElement(k - 1, i);
  }
}

lemma RangeSeqLength(a: int, b: int)
  ensures |RangeSeq(a, b)| == if a > b then 0 else b - a + 1
  decreases if b >= a then b - a + 1 else 0
{
  if a <= b { RangeSeqLength(a + 1, b); }
}

lemma RangeSeqAppend(a: int, b: int)
  requires a <= b
  ensures RangeSeq(a, b) == RangeSeq(a, b - 1) + [b]
  decreases b - a
{
  if a < b { RangeSeqAppend(a + 1, b); }
}

lemma InitialListEqualsRange(n: nat)
  ensures InitialList(n) == RangeSeq(1, n)
  decreases n
{
  if n > 0 {
    InitialListEqualsRange(n - 1);
    RangeSeqAppend(1, n);
  }
}

// Key lemma: simulating from a state [2,4,...,2k] ++ [2k+1,...,n] yields [2,4,...,2*(n/2)]
lemma SimulateFromState(k: nat, n: nat)
  requires 2 * k <= n
  ensures Simulate(EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n), k + 1) == EvenList(n / 2)
  decreases n - 2 * k
{
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(k)
  assert |EvenList(k)| == k;
  RangeSeqLength(2 * k + 1, n);
  var state := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
  if 2 * k == n {
    // Base: range is empty, step > |state|, Simulate returns state
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [];
  } else {
    // Inductive step: 2k < n, so step k+1 is valid
    assert |state| == n - k;
    assert k + 1 <= n - k;
    // Identify what's at index k (first element of the range suffix)
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [2 * k + 1] + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert state[..k] == EvenList(k);
    assert state[k..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
    assert state[k + 1..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    // After removing index k
    var afterRemoval := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert RemoveAtIndex(state, k) == afterRemoval;
    if 2 * (k + 1) > n {
      // n = 2k+1 (odd): range becomes empty
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k);
      assert n / 2 == k;
    } else {
      // 2(k+1) <= n: fold 2k+2 into the even prefix
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [2 * (k + 1)] + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      assert EvenList(k + 1) == EvenList(k) + [2 * (k + 1)];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k + 1) + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      SimulateFromState(k + 1, n);
    }
  }
}

lemma FinalListIsEven(n: nat)
  ensures FinalList(n) == EvenList(n / 2)
{
  InitialListEqualsRange(n);
  SimulateFromState(0, n);
}

method RemoveAProgression(n: int, x: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 1
  requires x >= 1
  requires x <= |FinalList(n)|
  ensures result == FinalList(n)[x - 1]
{
  // Inlined from FinalListIsEven(n)
  InitialListEqualsRange((n));

  SimulateFromState(0, (n));

  // Inlined from EvenListLength(n / 2)

  EvenListElement(n / 2, x - 1);
  return x * 2;
}

    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [2 * k + 1] + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert state[..k] == EvenList(k);
    assert state[k..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
    assert state[k + 1..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    // After removing index k
    var afterRemoval := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert RemoveAtIndex(state, k) == afterRemoval;
    if 2 * (k + 1) > n {
      // n = 2k+1 (odd): range becomes empty
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k);
      assert n / 2 == k;
    } else {
      // 2(k+1) <= n: fold 2k+2 into the even prefix
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [2 * (k + 1)] + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      assert EvenList(k + 1) == EvenList(k) + [2 * (k + 1)];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k + 1) + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      SimulateFromState(k + 1, n);
    }
  }
}

lemma FinalListIsEven(n: nat)
  ensures EvenList(n / 2) == FinalList(n)
{
  InitialListEqualsRange(n);
  SimulateFromState(0, n);
}

method RemoveAProgression(n: int, x: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 1
  requires x >= 1
  requires x <= |FinalList(n)|
  ensures result == FinalList(n)[x - 1]
{
  // Inlined from FinalListIsEven(n)
  InitialListEqualsRange((n));

  SimulateFromState(0, (n));

  // Inlined from EvenListLength(n / 2)

  EvenListElement(n / 2, x - 1);
  return x * 2;
}

  decreases n

// Key lemma: simulating from a state [2,4,...,2k] ++ [2k+1,...,n] yields [2,4,...,2*(n/2)]
lemma SimulateFromState(k: nat, n: nat)
  requires 2 * k <= n
  ensures Simulate(EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n), k + 1) == EvenList(n / 2)
  decreases n - 2 * k
{
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(k)
  assert |EvenList(k)| == k;
  RangeSeqLength(2 * k + 1, n);
  var state := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
  if 2 * k == n {
    // Base: range is empty, step > |state|, Simulate returns state
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [];
  } else {
    // Inductive step: 2k < n, so step k+1 is valid
    assert |state| == n - k;
    assert k + 1 <= n - k;
    // Identify what's at index k (first element of the range suffix)
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [2 * k + 1] + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert state[..k] == EvenList(k);
    assert state[k..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
    assert state[k + 1..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    // After removing index k
    var afterRemoval := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert RemoveAtIndex(state, k) == afterRemoval;
    if 2 * (k + 1) > n {
      // n = 2k+1 (odd): range becomes empty
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k);
      assert n / 2 == k;

      // 2(k+1) <= n: fold 2k+2 into the even prefix

      assert EvenList(k + 1) == EvenList(k) + [2 * (k + 1)];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k + 1) + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      SimulateFromState(k + 1, n);
    }
  }

  if i < k - 1 {
    EvenListElement(k - 1, i);
  }
}

lemma RangeSeqLength(a: int, b: int)
  ensures |RangeSeq(a, b)| == if a > b then 0 else b - a + 1
  decreases if b >= a then b - a + 1 else 0
{
  if a <= b { RangeSeqLength(a + 1, b); }
}

lemma RangeSeqAppend(a: int, b: int)
  requires a <= b
  ensures RangeSeq(a, b) == RangeSeq(a, b - 1) + [b]
  decreases b - a
{
  if a < b { RangeSeqAppend(a + 1, b); }
}

lemma InitialListEqualsRange(n: nat)
  ensures InitialList(n) == RangeSeq(1, n)
  decreases n
{
  if n > 0 {
    InitialListEqualsRange(n - 1);
    RangeSeqAppend(1, n);
  }
}

// Key lemma: simulating from a state [2,4,...,2k] ++ [2k+1,...,n] yields [2,4,...,2*(n/2)]
lemma SimulateFromState(k: nat, n: nat)
  requires 2 * k <= n
  ensures Simulate(EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n), k + 1) == EvenList(n / 2)
  decreases n - 2 * k
{
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(k)
  assert |EvenList(k)| == k;
  RangeSeqLength(2 * k + 1, n);
  var state := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
  if 2 * k == n {
    // Base: range is empty, step > |state|, Simulate returns state
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [];
  } else {
    // Inductive step: 2k < n, so step k+1 is valid
    assert |state| == n - k;
    assert k + 1 <= n - k;
    // Identify what's at index k (first element of the range suffix)
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [2 * k + 1] + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert state[..k] == EvenList(k);
    assert state[k..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
    assert state[k + 1..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    // After removing index k
    var afterRemoval := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert RemoveAtIndex(state, k) == afterRemoval;
    if 2 * (k + 1) > n {
      // n = 2k+1 (odd): range becomes empty
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k);
      assert n / 2 == k;
    } else {
      // 2(k+1) <= n: fold 2k+2 into the even prefix
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [2 * (k + 1)] + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      assert EvenList(k + 1) == EvenList(k) + [2 * (k + 1)];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k + 1) + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      SimulateFromState(k + 1, n);
    }
  }
}

lemma FinalListIsEven(n: nat)
  ensures FinalList(n) == EvenList(n / 2)
{
  // Inlined from InitialListEqualsRange
  InitialListEqualsRange(n);
  // Inlined from SimulateFromState
  SimulateFromState(0, n);
}

method RemoveAProgression(n: int, x: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 1
  requires x >= 1
  requires x <= |FinalList(n)|
  ensures result == FinalList(n)[x - 1]
{
  // Inlined from FinalListIsEven(n)
  InitialListEqualsRange((n));

  SimulateFromState(0, (n));

  // Inlined from EvenListLength(n / 2)

  EvenListElement(n / 2, x - 1);
  return x * 2;
}

lemma EvenListElement(k: nat, i: nat)
  requires i < k
  ensures |EvenList(k)| == k
  ensures EvenList(k)[i] == 2 * (i + 1)

  if i < k - 1 {

  }

lemma RangeSeqLength(a: int, b: int)
  ensures |RangeSeq(a, b)| == if a > b then 0 else b - a + 1
  decreases if b >= a then b - a + 1 else 0
{
  if a <= b { RangeSeqLength(a + 1, b); }
}

lemma RangeSeqAppend(a: int, b: int)
  requires a <= b
  ensures RangeSeq(a, b) == RangeSeq(a, b - 1) + [b]
  decreases b - a
{
  if a < b { RangeSeqAppend(a + 1, b); }
}

lemma InitialListEqualsRange(n: nat)
  ensures InitialList(n) == RangeSeq(1, n)
  decreases n
{
  if n > 0 {
    InitialListEqualsRange(n - 1);
    RangeSeqAppend(1, n);
  }
}

lemma SimulateFromState(k: nat, n: nat)
  requires 2 * k <= n
  ensures Simulate(EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n), k + 1) == EvenList(n / 2)
  decreases n - 2 * k
{
  assert |EvenList(k)| == k;
  RangeSeqLength(2 * k + 1, n);
  var state := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
  if 2 * k == n {
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [];
  } else {
    assert |state| == n - k;
    assert k + 1 <= n - k;
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [2 * k + 1] + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert state[..k] == EvenList(k);
    assert state[k..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
    assert state[k + 1..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    var afterRemoval := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert RemoveAtIndex(state, k) == afterRemoval;
    if 2 * (k + 1) > n {
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k);
      assert n / 2 == k;
    } else {
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [2 * (k + 1)] + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      assert EvenList(k + 1) == EvenList(k) + [2 * (k + 1)];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k + 1) + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      SimulateFromState(k + 1, n);
    }
  }
}

  ensures EvenList(n / 2) == FinalList(n)
{
  InitialListEqualsRange(n);
  SimulateFromState(0, n);
}

  requires x >= 1
  requires x <= |FinalList(n)|
  ensures result == FinalList(n)[x - 1]

  SimulateFromState(0, n);

  return x * 2;

// Key lemma: simulating from a state [2,4,...,2k] ++ [2k+1,...,n] yields [2,4,...,2*(n/2)]
lemma SimulateFromState(k: nat, n: nat)
  requires 2 * k <= n
  ensures Simulate(EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n), k + 1) == EvenList(n / 2)
  decreases n - 2 * k
{
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(k)
  assert |EvenList(k)| == k;
  RangeSeqLength(2 * k + 1, n);
  var state := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
  if 2 * k == n {
    // Base: range is empty, step > |state|, Simulate returns state
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [];
  } else {
    // Inductive step: 2k < n, so step k+1 is valid
    assert |state| == n - k;
    assert k + 1 <= n - k;
    // Identify what's at index k (first element of the range suffix)
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [2 * k + 1] + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert state[..k] == EvenList(k);
    assert state[k..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
    assert state[k + 1..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    // After removing index k
    var afterRemoval := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert RemoveAtIndex(state, k) == afterRemoval;
    if 2 * (k + 1) > n {
      // n = 2k+1 (odd): range becomes empty
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k);
      assert n / 2 == k;
    } else {
      // 2(k+1) <= n: fold 2k+2 into the even prefix
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [2 * (k + 1)] + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      assert EvenList(k + 1) == EvenList(k) + [2 * (k + 1)];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k + 1) + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      SimulateFromState(k + 1, n);
    }
  }
}

  InitialListEqualsRange(n);
  SimulateFromState(0, n);

ghost function EvenList(k: nat): seq<int>
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 then [] else EvenList(k - 1) + [2 * k]

ghost function RangeSeq(a: int, b: int): seq<int>

{

lemma EvenListElement(k: nat, i: nat)
  requires i < k
  ensures |EvenList(k)| == k
  ensures EvenList(k)[i] == 2 * (i + 1)
  decreases k
{
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(k)
  assert |EvenList(k)| == k;
  if i < k - 1 {
    EvenListElement(k - 1, i);
  }
}

lemma RangeSeqLength(a: int, b: int)
  ensures |RangeSeq(a, b)| == if a > b then 0 else b - a + 1
  decreases if b >= a then b - a + 1 else 0
{
  if a <= b { RangeSeqLength(a + 1, b); }
}

lemma RangeSeqAppend(a: int, b: int)
  requires a <= b
  ensures RangeSeq(a, b) == RangeSeq(a, b - 1) + [b]
  decreases b - a
{
  if a < b { RangeSeqAppend(a + 1, b); }
}

lemma InitialListEqualsRange(n: nat)
  ensures InitialList(n) == RangeSeq(1, n)
  decreases n
{
  if n > 0 {
    InitialListEqualsRange(n - 1);
    RangeSeqAppend(1, n);
  }
}

// Key lemma: simulating from a state [2,4,...,2k] ++ [2k+1,...,n] yields [2,4,...,2*(n/2)]
lemma SimulateFromState(k: nat, n: nat)
  requires 2 * k <= n
  ensures Simulate(EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n), k + 1) == EvenList(n / 2)
  decreases n - 2 * k
{
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(k)
  assert |EvenList(k)| == k;
  RangeSeqLength(2 * k + 1, n);
  var state := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
  if 2 * k == n {
    // Base: range is empty, step > |state|, Simulate returns state
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [];
    assert state == EvenList(k);
    assert Simulate(state, k + 1) == state;
    assert state == EvenList(k);
    assert EvenList(n / 2) == EvenList(k);
    assert Simulate(state, k + 1) == EvenList(k);
  } else {
    // Inductive step: 2k < n, so step k+1 is valid
    assert |state| == n - k;
    assert k + 1 <= n - k;
    // Identify what's at index k (first element of the range suffix)
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [2 * k + 1] + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert state[..k] == EvenList(k);
    assert state[k..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
    assert state[k + 1..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    // After removing index k
    var afterRemoval := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert RemoveAtIndex(state, k) == afterRemoval;
    if 2 * (k + 1) > n {
      // n = 2k+1 (odd): range becomes empty
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k);
      assert n / 2 == k;
      assert EvenList(n / 2) == EvenList(k);
      assert Simulate(afterRemoval, k + 2) == EvenList(k);
    } else {
      // 2(k+1) <= n: fold 2k+2 into the even prefix
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [2 * (k + 1)] + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      assert EvenList(k + 1) == EvenList(k) + [2 * (k + 1)];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k + 1) + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      SimulateFromState(k + 1, n);
    }
  }
}

lemma FinalListIsEven(n: nat)
  ensures FinalList(n) == EvenList(n / 2)
{
  InitialListEqualsRange(n);
  SimulateFromState(0, n);
}

method RemoveAProgression(n: int, x: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 1
  requires x >= 1
  requires x <= |FinalList(n)|
  ensures result == FinalList(n)[x - 1]
{
  // Inlined from FinalListIsEven(n)
  InitialListEqualsRange((n));

  SimulateFromState(0, (n));

  // Inlined from EvenListLength(n / 2)

  EvenListElement(n / 2, x - 1);
  return x * 2;
}

ghost function InitialList(n: nat): seq<int>
  decreases n
{
  if n == 0 then [] else InitialList(n - 1) + [n]
}

ghost function RemoveAtIndex(s: seq<int>, idx: nat): seq<int>
  requires idx < |s|
{
  s[..idx] + s[idx + 1..]
}

ghost function Simulate(remaining: seq<int>, step: nat): seq<int>
  decreases |remaining|
{
  if step == 0 || step > |remaining| then remaining
  else Simulate(RemoveAtIndex(remaining, step - 1), step + 1)

ghost function FinalList(n: nat): seq<int>
{
  Simulate(InitialList(n), 1)
}

// --- Proof infrastructure ---

ghost function EvenList(k: nat): seq<int>
  decreases k
{
  if k == 0 then [] else EvenList(k - 1) + [2 * k]
}

ghost function RangeSeq(a: int, b: int): seq<int>
  decreases if b >= a then b - a + 1 else 0
{
  if a > b then [] else [a] + RangeSeq(a + 1, b)
}

lemma EvenListElement(k: nat, i: nat)
  requires i < k
  ensures |EvenList(k)| == k
  ensures EvenList(k)[i] == 2 * (i + 1)
  decreases k
{
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(k)
  assert |EvenList(k)| == k;
  if i < k - 1 {
    EvenListElement(k - 1, i);
  }
}

lemma RangeSeqLength(a: int, b: int)
  ensures |RangeSeq(a, b)| == if a > b then 0 else b - a + 1
  decreases if b >= a then b - a + 1 else 0
{
  if a <= b { RangeSeqLength(a + 1, b); }
}

lemma RangeSeqAppend(a: int, b: int)
  requires a <= b
  ensures RangeSeq(a, b) == RangeSeq(a, b - 1) + [b]
  decreases b - a
{
  if a < b { RangeSeqAppend(a + 1, b); }
}

lemma InitialListEqualsRange(n: nat)
  ensures InitialList(n) == RangeSeq(1, n)
  decreases n
{
  if n > 0 {
    InitialListEqualsRange(n - 1);
    RangeSeqAppend(1, n);
  }
}

// Key lemma: simulating from a state [2,4,...,2k] ++ [2k+1,...,n] yields [2,4,...,2*(n/2)]
lemma SimulateFromState(k: nat, n: nat)
  requires 2 * k <= n
  ensures Simulate(EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n), k + 1) == EvenList(n / 2)
  decreases n - 2 * k
{
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(k)
  assert |EvenList(k)| == k;
  RangeSeqLength(2 * k + 1, n);
  var state := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
  if 2 * k == n {
    // Base: range is empty, step > |state|, Simulate returns state
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [];
    assert Simulate(state, k + 1) == EvenList(k);
    assert EvenList(n / 2) == EvenList(k);
  } else {
    // Inductive step: 2k < n, so step k+1 is valid
    assert |state| == n - k;
    assert k + 1 <= n - k;
    // Identify what's at index k (first element of the range suffix)
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [2 * k + 1] + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert state[..k] == EvenList(k);
    assert state[k..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
    assert state[k + 1..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    // After removing index k
    var afterRemoval := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert RemoveAtIndex(state, k) == afterRemoval;
    if 2 * (k + 1) > n {
      // n = 2k+1 (odd): range becomes empty
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k);
      assert n / 2 == k;
    } else {
      // 2(k+1) <= n: fold 2k+2 into the even prefix
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [2 * (k + 1)] + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      assert EvenList(k + 1) == EvenList(k) + [2 * (k + 1)];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k + 1) + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      SimulateFromState(k + 1, n);
    }
  }
}

lemma FinalListIsEven(n: nat)
  ensures |FinalList(n)| == n / 2
  ensures forall i :: 0 <= i < |FinalList(n)| ==> FinalList(n)[i] == 2 * (i + 1)
{
  InitialListEqualsRange(n);
  SimulateFromState(0, n);
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(n / 2)
  assert |EvenList(n / 2)| == n / 2;
  assert |FinalList(n)| == |EvenList(n / 2)|
  assert |FinalList(n)| == n / 2;
  // For the element-wise property, use EvenListElement
  var i := 0;
  while i < |FinalList(n)|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |FinalList(n)|
    invariant forall j :: 0 <= j < i ==> FinalList(n)[j] == 2 * (j + 1)
  {
    assert FinalList(n)[i] == EvenList(n / 2)[i];
    EvenListElement(n / 2, i);
    assert FinalList(n)[i] == 2 * (i + 1);
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

method RemoveAProgression(n: int, x: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 1
  requires x >= 1
  requires x <= |FinalList(n)|
  ensures result == FinalList(n)[x - 1]
{
  // Inlined from FinalListIsEven(n)
  InitialListEqualsRange((n));

  SimulateFromState(0, (n));

  // Inlined from EvenListLength(n / 2)

  EvenListElement(n / 2, x - 1);
  return x * 2;
}

    assert |state| == n - k;
    assert k + 1 <= n - k;
    // Identify what's at index k (first element of the range suffix)
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [2 * k + 1] + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert state[..k] == EvenList(k);
    assert state[k..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
    assert state[k + 1..] == RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    // After removing index k
    var afterRemoval := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n);
    assert RemoveAtIndex(state, k) == afterRemoval;
    if 2 * (k + 1) > n {
      // n = 2k+1 (odd): range becomes empty
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k);
      assert n / 2 == k;
    } else {
      // 2(k+1) <= n: fold 2k+2 into the even prefix
      assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 2, n) == [2 * (k + 1)] + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      assert EvenList(k + 1) == EvenList(k) + [2 * (k + 1)];
      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k + 1) + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      SimulateFromState(k + 1, n);
    }
  }
}

lemma FinalListIsEven(n: nat)
{
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(n / 2)
  assert |EvenList(n / 2)| == n / 2;
}

method RemoveAProgression(n: int, x: int) returns (result: int)
  requires n >= 1
  requires x >= 1
  requires x <= |FinalList(n)|
  ensures result == FinalList(n)[x - 1]
{
  // Inlined from FinalListIsEven(n)
  InitialListEqualsRange((n));

  SimulateFromState(0, (n));

  // Inlined from EvenListLength(n / 2)

  EvenListElement(n / 2, x - 1);
  return x * 2;

// Key lemma: simulating from a state [2,4,...,2k] ++ [2k+1,...,n] yields [2,4,...,2*(n/2)]
lemma SimulateFromState(k: nat, n: nat)
  requires 2 * k <= n
  ensures Simulate(EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n), k + 1) == EvenList(n / 2)
  decreases n - 2 * k
{
  // Inlined from EvenListLength(k)
  assert |EvenList(k)| == k;
  RangeSeqLength(2 * k + 1, n);
  var state := EvenList(k) + RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n);
  if 2 * k == n {
    // Base: range is empty, step > |state|, Simulate returns state
    assert RangeSeq(2 * k + 1, n) == [];
  } else {
    // Inductive step: 2k < n, so step k+1 is valid

    assert k + 1 <= n - k;

    assert RemoveAtIndex(state, k) == afterRemoval;

      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k);

      assert afterRemoval == EvenList(k + 1) + RangeSeq(2 * (k + 1) + 1, n);
      SimulateFromState(k + 1, n);
    }
  }
